layout: "post"
title: "The circle"
date: "2018-05-01"
agda: true
toc: true
categories: type-theory
---

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: . equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

I gave a talk giving one solution using the flattening lemma:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="616" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="621" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="628" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">2018-07-06-mini-hott</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  S¹ type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point
and one no trivial path called path as we show in the following
picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png)
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

## `pS` type

![path](/assets/ipe-images/tour-type.png)
*Figure 2. `pS` Type.*

## Equivalences

### Lemma 1

{: .equation }

  $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**.

Let us define the outgoing functions:

<a id="3989" class="Keyword">private</a>

The proof of the homotopy $$ f' ∘ g' \sim \mathsf{id}$$.

          <a id="8388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#5177" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="8393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#2058" class="Function">pS₀</a>
        <a id="8405" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7523" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of the homotopy $$g' ∘ f' \sim \mathsf{id}$$:

### Lemma 2

- Action on paths of pairs

### Lemma 3

{: .equation}
  $$
    \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS
  $$

  where $$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

            <a id="14051" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7424" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="14055" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#23883" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="14062" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="14065" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14066" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#14066" class="Bound">pb</a> <a id="14069" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14071" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#11894" class="Function">P</a> <a id="14073" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#961" class="Function">base</a><a id="14077" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14079" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14081" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7800" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="14084" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13290" class="Function">d̰</a> <a id="14087" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14088" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12601" class="Function">aux-lemma₁</a> <a id="14099" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#14066" class="Bound">pb</a><a id="14101" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14104" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7424" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
          <a id="14116" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="14119" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14120" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#14120" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14122" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14124" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#11894" class="Function">P</a> <a id="14126" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#961" class="Function">base</a><a id="14130" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14132" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14134" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13290" class="Function">d̰</a> <a id="14137" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14138" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#11717" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="14142" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#14120" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14143" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14145" class="Symbol">)</a>
            <a id="14159" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7424" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="14163" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#23883" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="14170" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="14173" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#14173" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="14175" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14177" class="Symbol">{!   !})</a>  <a id="14187" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7424" class="Function Operator">⟩</a> <a id="14189" class="Comment">-- I got stuck here.</a>
          <a id="14220" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13290" class="Function">d̰</a>
         <a id="14232" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7523" class="Function Operator">∎</a>

<a id="14235" class="Comment">-- ΣSP-≃-pS : Σ S¹ P ≃ pS</a>
<a id="14261" class="Comment">-- ΣSP-≃-pS = qinv-≃ f {!   !}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14319" class="Comment">-- -- Defs.</a>
<a id="14331" class="Comment">--     γ₀₁   = transport-ua P loop neg-eq (S¹-βrec Type₀ Bool (ua neg-eq)) false</a>
<a id="14412" class="Comment">--     g-p₀₁ = pair= (loop , γ₀₁)</a>
<a id="14446" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="14449" class="Comment">--     γ₁₀   = transport-ua P loop neg-eq (S¹-βrec Type₀ Bool (ua neg-eq)) true</a>
<a id="14529" class="Comment">--     g-p₁₀ = pair= (loop , γ₁₀)</a>
<a id="14563" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="14566" class="Comment">--     g : pS → Σ S¹ P</a>
<a id="14589" class="Comment">--     g = -- 0   ↦ (base, 0)</a>
<a id="14619" class="Comment">--         -- 1   ↦ (base, 1)</a>
<a id="14649" class="Comment">--         -- p₀₁ ↦ (base, 0) == (base, 1)</a>
<a id="14692" class="Comment">--         -- p₁₀ ↦ (base, 1) == (base, 0)</a>
<a id="14735" class="Comment">--         pS-rec</a>
<a id="14753" class="Comment">--             (Σ S¹ P)</a>
<a id="14777" class="Comment">--             (base , false)</a>
<a id="14807" class="Comment">--             (base , true)</a>
<a id="14836" class="Comment">--             g-p₀₁</a>
<a id="14857" class="Comment">--             g-p₁₀</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14903" class="Comment">-- -- Missing lemmas.</a>
<a id="14925" class="Comment">--     postulate</a>
<a id="14942" class="Comment">--       lemma-ap-f-γ₀₁ : ap f (pair= (loop , γ₀₁)) == p₀₁</a>
<a id="15001" class="Comment">--       lemma-ap-f-γ₁₀ : ap f (pair= (loop , γ₁₀)) == p₁₀</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Let us prove the homotopies:
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15114" class="Comment">-- Homotopy</a>
    <a id="15130" class="Comment">-- f-g : f ∘ g ∼ id</a>
    <a id="15154" class="Comment">-- f-g = pS-ind (λ ps → (f ∘ g) ps == id ps) q₀ q₁ dpath₁ dpath₂</a>
    <a id="15223" class="Comment">--   where</a>
    <a id="15238" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="15245" class="Comment">--     q₀ : (f ∘ g) pS₀ == id pS₀</a>
    <a id="15283" class="Comment">--     q₀ = p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15303" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="15310" class="Comment">--     q₁ : (f ∘ g) pS₁ == id pS₁</a>
    <a id="15348" class="Comment">--     q₁ = p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15368" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="15375" class="Comment">--     dpath₁ :  q₀ == q₁ [ (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) ↓ p₀₁ ]</a>
    <a id="15441" class="Comment">--     dpath₁ =</a>
    <a id="15461" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
    <a id="15480" class="Comment">--         transport (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) p₀₁ q₀</a>
    <a id="15538" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ transport-eq-fun (f ∘ g) id p₀₁ q₀ ⟩</a>
    <a id="15596" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₀₁ · q₀ · ap id p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15645" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (! ap (f ∘ g) p₀₁ · q₀ ·_) (ap-id p₀₁) ⟩</a>
    <a id="15710" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₀₁ · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15753" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₀ · p₀₁) (! ap-comp g f p₀₁) ⟩</a>
    <a id="15822" class="Comment">--         ! ap f (ap g p₀₁) · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15866" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! ap f r · q₀ · p₀₁)</a>
    <a id="15918" class="Comment">--                  (pS-βrec₀₁ ((Σ S¹ (λ b → P b))) (base , false) (base , true) g-p₀₁ g-p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16018" class="Comment">--         ! ap f g-p₀₁ · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="16057" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₀ · p₀₁) lemma-ap-f-γ₀₁ ⟩</a>
    <a id="16121" class="Comment">--         ! p₁₀ · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="16153" class="Comment">--           ==⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="16175" class="Comment">--         ! p₁₀ · p₁₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="16208" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (_· p₀₁) (·-linv p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16256" class="Comment">--         idp · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="16281" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ·-lunit p₀₁ ⟩</a>
    <a id="16316" class="Comment">--         q₁</a>
    <a id="16334" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
    <a id="16349" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="16356" class="Comment">--     dpath₂ : q₁ == q₀ [ (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) ↓ p₁₀ ]</a>
    <a id="16421" class="Comment">--     dpath₂ =</a>
    <a id="16441" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
    <a id="16460" class="Comment">--         transport (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) p₁₀ q₁</a>
    <a id="16518" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ transport-eq-fun (f ∘ g) id p₁₀ q₁ ⟩</a>
    <a id="16576" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₁₀ · q₁ · ap id p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16625" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (! ap (f ∘ g) p₁₀ · q₁ ·_) (ap-id p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16690" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₁₀ · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16733" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₁ · p₁₀) (! ap-comp g f p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16802" class="Comment">--         ! ap f (ap g p₁₀) · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16846" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! ap f r · q₁ · p₁₀)</a>
    <a id="16898" class="Comment">--                  (pS-βrec₁₀ ((Σ S¹ (λ b → P b))) (base , false) (base , true) g-p₀₁ g-p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16998" class="Comment">--         ! ap f g-p₁₀ · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="17037" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₁ · p₁₀) lemma-ap-f-γ₁₀ ⟩</a>
    <a id="17101" class="Comment">--         ! p₀₁ · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="17133" class="Comment">--           ==⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="17155" class="Comment">--         ! p₀₁ · p₀₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="17188" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (_· p₁₀) (·-linv p₀₁) ⟩</a>
    <a id="17236" class="Comment">--         idp · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="17261" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ·-lunit p₁₀ ⟩</a>
    <a id="17296" class="Comment">--         q₀</a>
    <a id="17314" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17350" class="Comment">-- -- Homotopy</a>
<a id="17365" class="Comment">--     g-f : g ∘ f ∼ id</a>
<a id="17389" class="Comment">--     g-f (s , pₛ) = g-f&#39; s pₛ</a>
<a id="17421" class="Comment">--       where</a>
